                  <script>
                   function SetTitle() {

            var $this = $('#ContentPlaceHolderBase_ContentPlaceHolder1_ucSubscribe_txbSubscr');

            if ($this.val() === '') {
                $this.val($this.attr('title'));
            }
            $this.focus(function () {
                if ($this.val() === $this.attr('title')) {
                    $this.val('');
                }
            });
            $this.blur(function () {
                if ($this.val() === '') {
                    $this.val($this.attr('title'));
                }
            });

            

        }
